               </div>
               Ever get bored
               <i>
                completely on your own time
               </i>
               ? Before 8:00
               <i>
                pm
               </i>
               ? Boy, I did today, so I figured I would improve game boxes with googly eyes.
               <br/>
               <br/>
               And don't let me have the only fun with this, here's your own googly eye to submit your own!
               <br/>
               <br/>
               <div>
                <a href="/image/1582363">
                 <img onload="ImageResizer.resize(this);" src="//cf.geekdo-images.com/images/pic1582363_t.png"/>
                </a>

               <br/>
               Edited purely for CYA.

               </a>

                I'm just not sure I trust this vendor - there's something I don't like about how he's looking at me.
